| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2920">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2920">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2921">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2921">2</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2922">Hint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2922">Hint</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2923">Um índice na tabela de ponteiros do nome de exportação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2923">An index into the export name pointer table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2924">Uma correspondência é tentada primeiro com esse valor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2924">A match is attempted first with this value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2925">Se falhar, uma pesquisa binária será executada na tabela de ponteiro de nome de exportação da DLL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2925">If it fails, a binary search is performed on the DLL's export name pointer table.</span></span> <br/>            |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2926">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2926">2</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2927">variável</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2927">variable</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2928">Nome</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2928">Name</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2929">Uma cadeia de caracteres ASCII que contém o nome a ser importado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2929">An ASCII string that contains the name to import.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2930">Essa é a cadeia de caracteres que deve ser correspondida ao nome público na DLL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2930">This is the string that must be matched to the public name in the DLL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2931">Essa cadeia de caracteres diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas e terminada por um byte nulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2931">This string is case sensitive and terminated by a null byte.</span></span> <br/> |
| \* <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2932">0 ou 1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2932">0 or 1</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2933">Pad</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2933">Pad</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2934">Um byte de teclado zero à direita que aparece após o byte nulo à direita, se necessário, para alinhar a próxima entrada em um limite par.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2934">A trailing zero-pad byte that appears after the trailing null byte, if necessary, to align the next entry on an even boundary.</span></span> <br/>                                                        |



 

#### <a name="import-address-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2935">Importar tabela de endereços</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2935">Import Address Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2936">A estrutura e o conteúdo da tabela de endereços de importação são idênticos aos da tabela de pesquisa de importação, até que o arquivo esteja associado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2936">The structure and content of the import address table are identical to those of the import lookup table, until the file is bound.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2937">Durante a associação, as entradas na tabela de endereços de importação são substituídas pelos endereços de 32 bits (para PE32) ou 64 bits (para PE32 +) dos símbolos que estão sendo importados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2937">During binding, the entries in the import address table are overwritten with the 32-bit (for PE32) or 64-bit (for PE32+) addresses of the symbols that are being imported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2938">Esses endereços são os endereços de memória reais dos símbolos, embora tecnicamente eles ainda sejam chamados de "endereços virtuais".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2938">These addresses are the actual memory addresses of the symbols, although technically they are still called "virtual addresses."</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2939">O carregador normalmente processa a associação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2939">The loader typically processes the binding.</span></span>

### <a name="the-pdata-section"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2940">A seção. pData</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2940">The .pdata Section</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2941">A seção. pData contém uma matriz de entradas de tabela de função que são usadas para manipulação de exceção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2941">The .pdata section contains an array of function table entries that are used for exception handling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2942">Ele é apontado pela entrada da tabela de exceção no diretório de dados de imagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2942">It is pointed to by the exception table entry in the image data directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2943">As entradas devem ser classificadas de acordo com os endereços de função (o primeiro campo em cada estrutura) antes de serem emitidas na imagem final.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2943">The entries must be sorted according to the function addresses (the first field in each structure) before being emitted into the final image.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2944">A plataforma de destino determina quais das três variações de formato de entrada de tabela de função descritas abaixo são usadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2944">The target platform determines which of the three function table entry format variations described below is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2945">Para imagens MIPS de 32 bits, as entradas da tabela de funções têm o seguinte formato:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2945">For 32-bit MIPS images, function table entries have the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2946">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2946">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2947">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2947">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2948">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2948">Field</span></span>                          | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2949">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2949">Description</span></span>                                                                    |
|----------------|---------------|--------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2950">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2950">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2951">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2951">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2952">Endereço inicial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2952">Begin Address</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2953">O VA da função correspondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2953">The VA of the corresponding function.</span></span> <br/>                              |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2954">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2954">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2955">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2955">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2956">Endereço final</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2956">End Address</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2957">O VA do final da função.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2957">The VA of the end of the function.</span></span> <br/>                                 |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2958">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2958">8</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2959">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2959">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2960">Manipulador de exceção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2960">Exception Handler</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2961">O ponteiro para o manipulador de exceção a ser executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2961">The pointer to the exception handler to be executed.</span></span> <br/>               |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2962">12</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2962">12</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2963">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2963">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2964">Dados do manipulador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2964">Handler Data</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2965">O ponteiro para informações adicionais a serem passadas para o manipulador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2965">The pointer to additional information to be passed to the handler.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2966">16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2966">16</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2967">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2967">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2968">Endereço final do prólogo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2968">Prolog End Address</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2969">O VA do final do prólogo da função.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2969">The VA of the end of the function's prolog.</span></span> <br/>                        |



 

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2970">Para as plataformas ARM, PowerPC, SH3 e SH4 Windows CE, as entradas da tabela de funções têm o seguinte formato:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2970">For the ARM, PowerPC, SH3 and SH4 Windows CE platforms, function table entries have the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2971">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2971">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2972">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2972">Size</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2973">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2973">Field</span></span>                       | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2974">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2974">Description</span></span>                                                                                                               |
|---------------|---------------------|-----------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2975">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2975">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2976">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2976">4</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2977">Endereço inicial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2977">Begin Address</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2978">O VA da função correspondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2978">The VA of the corresponding function.</span></span> <br/>                                                                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2979">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2979">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2980">8 bits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2980">8 bits</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2981">Comprimento do prólogo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2981">Prolog Length</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2982">O número de instruções no prólogo da função.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2982">The number of instructions in the function's prolog.</span></span> <br/>                                                          |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2983">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2983">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2984">22 bits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2984">22 bits</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2985">Comprimento da função</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2985">Function Length</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2986">O número de instruções na função.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2986">The number of instructions in the function.</span></span> <br/>                                                                   |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2987">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2987">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2988">1 bit</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2988">1 bit</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2989">Sinalizador de 32 bits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2989">32-bit Flag</span></span> <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2990">Se definido, a função consiste em instruções de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2990">If set, the function consists of 32-bit instructions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2991">Se claro, a função consiste em instruções de 16 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2991">If clear, the function consists of 16-bit instructions.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2992">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2992">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2993">1 bit</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2993">1 bit</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2994">Sinalizador de exceção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2994">Exception Flag</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2995">Se definido, existe um manipulador de exceção para a função.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2995">If set, an exception handler exists for the function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2996">Caso contrário, não existe nenhum manipulador de exceção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2996">Otherwise, no exception handler exists.</span></span> <br/>                 |



 

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2997">Para plataformas x64 e Itanium, as entradas da tabela de funções têm o seguinte formato:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2997">For x64 and Itanium platforms, function table entries have the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2998">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2998">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-2999">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-2999">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3000">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3000">Field</span></span>                          | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3001">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3001">Description</span></span>                                        |
|---------------|---------------|--------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3002">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3002">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3003">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3003">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3004">Endereço inicial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3004">Begin Address</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3005">O RVA da função correspondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3005">The RVA of the corresponding function.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3006">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3006">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3007">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3007">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3008">Endereço final</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3008">End Address</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3009">O RVA do final da função.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3009">The RVA of the end of the function.</span></span> <br/>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3010">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3010">8</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3011">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3011">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3012">Informações de desenrolamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3012">Unwind Information</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3013">O RVA das informações de desenrolamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3013">The RVA of the unwind information.</span></span> <br/>     |



 

### <a name="the-reloc-section-image-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3014">A seção. realocação (somente imagem)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3014">The .reloc Section (Image Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3015">A tabela de realocação base contém entradas para todas as realocações de base na imagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3015">The base relocation table contains entries for all base relocations in the image.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3016">O campo tabela de realocação base nos diretórios de dados de cabeçalho opcionais fornece o número de bytes na tabela de realocação base.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3016">The Base Relocation Table field in the optional header data directories gives the number of bytes in the base relocation table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3017">Para obter mais informações, consulte [diretórios de dados de cabeçalho opcionais (somente imagem)](#optional-header-data-directories-image-only).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3017">For more information, see [Optional Header Data Directories (Image Only)](#optional-header-data-directories-image-only).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3018">A tabela de realocação base é dividida em blocos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3018">The base relocation table is divided into blocks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3019">Cada bloco representa as realocações de base para uma página de 4K.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3019">Each block represents the base relocations for a 4K page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3020">Cada bloco deve iniciar em um limite de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3020">Each block must start on a 32-bit boundary.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3021">O carregador não é necessário para processar as relocalidades de base que são resolvidas pelo vinculador, a menos que a imagem de carga não possa ser carregada na base da imagem especificada no cabeçalho PE.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3021">The loader is not required to process base relocations that are resolved by the linker, unless the load image cannot be loaded at the image base that is specified in the PE header.</span></span>

#### <a name="base-relocation-block"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3022">Bloco de realocação de base</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3022">Base Relocation Block</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3023">Cada bloco de realocação de base começa com a seguinte estrutura:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3023">Each base relocation block starts with the following structure:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3024">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3024">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3025">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3025">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3026">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3026">Field</span></span>                  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3027">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3027">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                              |
|---------------|---------------|------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3028">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3028">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3029">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3029">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3030">RVA da página</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3030">Page RVA</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3031">A imagem base mais a página RVA é adicionada a cada deslocamento para criar o VA em que a realocação de base deve ser aplicada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3031">The image base plus the page RVA is added to each offset to create the VA where the base relocation must be applied.</span></span> <br/>                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3032">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3032">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3033">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3033">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3034">Tamanho do bloco</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3034">Block Size</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3035">O número total de bytes no bloco de realocação de base, incluindo os campos RVA da página e tamanho do bloco e os campos tipo/deslocamento a seguir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3035">The total number of bytes in the base relocation block, including the Page RVA and Block Size fields and the Type/Offset fields that follow.</span></span> <br/> |



 

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3036">O campo tamanho do bloco é seguido por qualquer número de entradas de campo de tipo ou deslocamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3036">The Block Size field is then followed by any number of Type or Offset field entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3037">Cada entrada é uma palavra (2 bytes) e tem a seguinte estrutura:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3037">Each entry is a WORD (2 bytes) and has the following structure:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3038">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3038">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3039">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3039">Size</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3040">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3040">Field</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3041">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3041">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
|---------------|---------------------|--------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3042">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3042">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3043">4 bits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3043">4 bits</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3044">Tipo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3044">Type</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3045">Armazenados nos quatro bits superiores da palavra, um valor que indica o tipo de realocação de base a ser aplicado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3045">Stored in the high 4 bits of the WORD, a value that indicates the type of base relocation to be applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3046">Para obter mais informações, consulte [base de tipos de realocação](#base-relocation-types).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3046">For more information, see [Base Relocation Types](#base-relocation-types).</span></span><br/>                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3047">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3047">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3048">12 bits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3048">12 bits</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3049">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3049">Offset</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3050">Armazenados nos 12 bits restantes da palavra, um deslocamento do endereço inicial que foi especificado no campo RVA da página para o bloco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3050">Stored in the remaining 12 bits of the WORD, an offset from the starting address that was specified in the Page RVA field for the block.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3051">Esse deslocamento especifica onde a realocação de base deve ser aplicada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3051">This offset specifies where the base relocation is to be applied.</span></span> <br/> |



 

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3052">Para aplicar uma realocação de base, a diferença é calculada entre o endereço base preferencial e a base em que a imagem é realmente carregada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3052">To apply a base relocation, the difference is calculated between the preferred base address and the base where the image is actually loaded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3053">Se a imagem for carregada em sua base preferida, a diferença será zero e, portanto, as realocações básicas não precisarão ser aplicadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3053">If the image is loaded at its preferred base, the difference is zero and thus the base relocations do not have to be applied.</span></span>

#### <a name="base-relocation-types"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3054">Tipos de realocação base</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3054">Base Relocation Types</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3055">Constante</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3055">Constant</span></span>                                       | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3056">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3056">Value</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3057">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3057">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
|------------------------------------------------|----------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3058">\_ \_ absoluto com base em rel de imagem \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3058">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_ABSOLUTE</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3059">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3059">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3060">A realocação de base é ignorada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3060">The base relocation is skipped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3061">Esse tipo pode ser usado para preencher um bloco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3061">This type can be used to pad a block.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3062">\_ \_ com base em rel de imagem \_ alta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3062">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_HIGH</span></span> <br/>            | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3063">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3063">1</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3064">A realocação de base adiciona os 16 bits superiores da diferença ao campo de 16 bits no deslocamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3064">The base relocation adds the high 16 bits of the difference to the 16-bit field at offset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3065">O campo de 16 bits representa o valor alto de uma palavra de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3065">The 16-bit field represents the high value of a 32-bit word.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                               |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3066">\_com base em rel. de imagem \_ \_ baixa</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3066">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_LOW</span></span> <br/>             | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3067">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3067">2</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3068">A realocação de base adiciona os 16 bits baixos da diferença ao campo de 16 bits no deslocamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3068">The base relocation adds the low 16 bits of the difference to the 16-bit field at offset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3069">O campo de 16 bits representa a metade inferior de uma palavra de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3069">The 16-bit field represents the low half of a 32-bit word.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                  |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3070">\_ \_ HIGHLOW com base em rel de imagem \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3070">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_HIGHLOW</span></span> <br/>         | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3071">3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3071">3</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3072">A realocação de base aplica todos os 32 bits da diferença ao campo de 32 bits no deslocamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3072">The base relocation applies all 32 bits of the difference to the 32-bit field at offset.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3073">\_ \_ HIGHADJ com base em rel de imagem \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3073">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_HIGHADJ</span></span> <br/>         | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3074">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3074">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3075">A realocação de base adiciona os 16 bits superiores da diferença ao campo de 16 bits no deslocamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3075">The base relocation adds the high 16 bits of the difference to the 16-bit field at offset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3076">O campo de 16 bits representa o valor alto de uma palavra de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3076">The 16-bit field represents the high value of a 32-bit word.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3077">Os 16 bits baixos do valor de 32 bits são armazenados na palavra de 16 bits que segue essa realocação base.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3077">The low 16 bits of the 32-bit value are stored in the 16-bit word that follows this base relocation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3078">Isso significa que essa realocação básica ocupa dois slots.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3078">This means that this base relocation occupies two slots.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3079">\_ \_ JMPADDR MIPS baseada em rel \_ de \_ imagem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3079">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_MIPS\_JMPADDR</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3080">5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3080">5</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3081">A interpretação de realocação depende do tipo de computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3081">The relocation interpretation is dependent on the machine type.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3082">Quando o tipo de computador é MIPS, a realocação de base se aplica a uma instrução de salto de MIPS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3082">When the machine type is MIPS, the base relocation applies to a MIPS jump instruction.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                    |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3083">\_ \_ MOV32 ARM baseado em rel \_ de \_ imagem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3083">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_ARM\_MOV32</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3084">5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3084">5</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3085">Essa relocação só é significativa quando o tipo de computador é ARM ou Thumb.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3085">This relocation is meaningful only when the machine type is ARM or Thumb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3086">A realocação de base aplica o endereço de 32 bits de um símbolo em um par de instruções MOVW/MOVT consecutivas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3086">The base relocation applies the 32-bit address of a symbol across a consecutive MOVW/MOVT instruction pair.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                 |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3087">\_ \_ \_ RISCV HIGH20 com base em rel de imagem \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3087">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_RISCV\_HIGH20</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3088">5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3088">5</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3089">Essa relocação só é significativa quando o tipo de computador é RISC-V.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3089">This relocation is only meaningful when the machine type is RISC-V.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3090">A realocação de base aplica-se aos altos 20 bits de um endereço absoluto de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3090">The base relocation applies to the high 20 bits of a 32-bit absolute address.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                     |
|                                                | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3091">6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3091">6</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3092">Reservado, deve ser zero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3092">Reserved, must be zero.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3093">\_ \_ MOV32 Thumb com base em rel de imagem \_ \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3093">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_THUMB\_MOV32</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3094">7</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3094">7</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3095">Essa relocação só é significativa quando o tipo de computador é Thumb.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3095">This relocation is meaningful only when the machine type is Thumb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3096">A realocação de base aplica o endereço de 32 bits de um símbolo a um par de instruções MOVW/MOVT consecutivas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3096">The base relocation applies the 32-bit address of a symbol to a consecutive MOVW/MOVT instruction pair.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3097">\_ \_ \_ RISCV LOW12I com base em rel de imagem \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3097">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_RISCV\_LOW12I</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3098">7</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3098">7</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3099">Essa relocação só é significativa quando o tipo de computador é RISC-V.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3099">This relocation is only meaningful when the machine type is RISC-V.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3100">A realocação de base aplica-se aos 12 bits baixos de um endereço absoluto de 32 bits formado em formato de instrução de tipo RISC-V.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3100">The base relocation applies to the low 12 bits of a 32-bit absolute address formed in RISC-V I-type instruction format.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                           |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3101">\_ \_ \_ RISCV LOW12S com base em rel de imagem \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3101">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_RISCV\_LOW12S</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3102">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3102">8</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3103">Essa relocação só é significativa quando o tipo de computador é RISC-V.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3103">This relocation is only meaningful when the machine type is RISC-V.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3104">A realocação de base aplica-se aos 12 bits baixos de um endereço absoluto de 32 bits formado no formato de instrução RISC-V S-Type.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3104">The base relocation applies to the low 12 bits of a 32-bit absolute address formed in RISC-V S-type instruction format.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                           |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3105">\_ \_ JMPADDR16 MIPS baseada em rel \_ de \_ imagem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3105">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_MIPS\_JMPADDR16</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3106">9</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3106">9</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3107">A realocação só é significativa quando o tipo de computador é MIPS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3107">The relocation is only meaningful when the machine type is MIPS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3108">A realocação de base se aplica a uma instrução de salto MIPS16.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3108">The base relocation applies to a MIPS16 jump instruction.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3109">\_ \_ DIR64 com base em rel de imagem \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3109">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_DIR64</span></span> <br/>           | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3110">10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3110">10</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3111">A realocação de base aplica a diferença ao campo de 64 bits no deslocamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3111">The base relocation applies the difference to the 64-bit field at offset.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |



 

### <a name="the-tls-section"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3112">A seção. TLS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3112">The .tls Section</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3113">A seção. TLS fornece suporte direto a PE e COFF para o armazenamento local de thread estático (TLS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3113">The .tls section provides direct PE and COFF support for static thread local storage (TLS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3114">O TLS é uma classe de armazenamento especial que o Windows dá suporte no, em que um objeto de dados não é uma variável automática (pilha), mas é local para cada thread individual que executa o código.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3114">TLS is a special storage class that Windows supports in which a data object is not an automatic (stack) variable, yet is local to each individual thread that runs the code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3115">Assim, cada thread pode manter um valor diferente para uma variável declarada usando TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3115">Thus, each thread can maintain a different value for a variable declared by using TLS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3116">Observe que qualquer quantidade de dados TLS pode ser suportada usando as chamadas de API TlsAlloc, TlsFree, TlsSetValue e TlsGetValue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3116">Note that any amount of TLS data can be supported by using the API calls TlsAlloc, TlsFree, TlsSetValue, and TlsGetValue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3117">A implementação de PE ou COFF é uma abordagem alternativa para usar a API e tem a vantagem de ser mais simples do ponto de vista do programador de linguagem de alto nível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3117">The PE or COFF implementation is an alternative approach to using the API and has the advantage of being simpler from the high-level-language programmer's viewpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3118">Essa implementação permite que os dados TLS sejam definidos e inicializados da mesma forma que as variáveis estáticas comuns em um programa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3118">This implementation enables TLS data to be defined and initialized similarly to ordinary static variables in a program.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3119">Por exemplo, no Visual C++, uma variável TLS estática pode ser definida da seguinte maneira, sem usar a API do Windows:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3119">For example, in Visual C++, a static TLS variable can be defined as follows, without using the Windows API:</span></span>

`__declspec (thread) int tlsFlag = 1;`

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3120">Para dar suporte a essa construção de programação, a seção PE e COFF. TLS especifica as seguintes informações: dados de inicialização, rotinas de retorno de chamada para a inicialização e encerramento por thread e o índice TLS, que são explicados na discussão a seguir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3120">To support this programming construct, the PE and COFF .tls section specifies the following information: initialization data, callback routines for per-thread initialization and termination, and the TLS index, which are explained in the following discussion.</span></span>

> [!Note]
>
> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3121">Os objetos de dados TLS declarados estaticamente podem ser usados somente em arquivos de imagem carregados estaticamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3121">Statically declared TLS data objects can be used only in statically loaded image files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3122">Esse fato torna não confiável usar dados TLS estáticos em uma DLL, a menos que você saiba que a DLL ou qualquer coisa vinculada estaticamente a ela nunca será carregada dinamicamente com a função de API LoadLibrary.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3122">This fact makes it unreliable to use static TLS data in a DLL unless you know that the DLL, or anything statically linked with it, will never be loaded dynamically with the LoadLibrary API function.</span></span>

 

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3123">O código executável acessa um objeto de dados TLS estático por meio das seguintes etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3123">Executable code accesses a static TLS data object through the following steps:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3124">No momento do link, o vinculador define o endereço do campo de índice do diretório TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3124">At link time, the linker sets the Address of Index field of the TLS directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3125">Esse campo aponta para um local em que o programa espera receber o índice TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3125">This field points to a location where the program expects to receive the TLS index.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3126">A biblioteca de tempo de execução da Microsoft facilita esse processo definindo uma imagem de memória do diretório TLS e dando a ela o nome especial " \_ \_ TLS \_ usado" (plataformas Intel x86) ou " \_ TLS \_ usado" (outras plataformas).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3126">The Microsoft run-time library facilitates this process by defining a memory image of the TLS directory and giving it the special name "\_\_tls\_used" (Intel x86 platforms) or "\_tls\_used" (other platforms).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3127">O vinculador procura essa imagem de memória e usa os dados ali para criar o diretório TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3127">The linker looks for this memory image and uses the data there to create the TLS directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3128">Outros compiladores que dão suporte a TLS e trabalham com o vinculador da Microsoft devem usar essa mesma técnica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3128">Other compilers that support TLS and work with the Microsoft linker must use this same technique.</span></span>

2.  <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3129">Quando um thread é criado, o carregador comunica o endereço da matriz TLS do thread, colocando o endereço do bloco de ambiente de thread (TEB) no registro FS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3129">When a thread is created, the loader communicates the address of the thread's TLS array by placing the address of the thread environment block (TEB) in the FS register.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3130">Um ponteiro para a matriz TLS está no deslocamento de 0x2C do início de TEB.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3130">A pointer to the TLS array is at the offset of 0x2C from the beginning of TEB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3131">Esse comportamento é específico do Intel x86.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3131">This behavior is Intel x86-specific.</span></span>

3.  <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3132">O carregador atribui o valor do índice TLS ao local indicado pelo endereço do campo de índice.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3132">The loader assigns the value of the TLS index to the place that was indicated by the Address of Index field.</span></span>

4.  <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3133">O código executável recupera o índice TLS e também o local da matriz TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3133">The executable code retrieves the TLS index and also the location of the TLS array.</span></span>

5.  <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3134">O código usa o índice TLS e o local da matriz TLS (multiplicando o índice por 4 e usando-o como um deslocamento para a matriz) para obter o endereço da área de dados TLS para o programa e o módulo especificados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3134">The code uses the TLS index and the TLS array location (multiplying the index by 4 and using it as an offset to the array) to get the address of the TLS data area for the given program and module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3135">Cada thread tem sua própria área de dados TLS, mas isso é transparente para o programa, que não precisa saber como os dados são alocados para threads individuais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3135">Each thread has its own TLS data area, but this is transparent to the program, which does not need to know how data is allocated for individual threads.</span></span>

6.  <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3136">Um objeto de dados TLS individual é acessado como um deslocamento fixo na área de dados TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3136">An individual TLS data object is accessed as some fixed offset into the TLS data area.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3137">A matriz TLS é uma matriz de endereços que o sistema mantém para cada thread.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3137">The TLS array is an array of addresses that the system maintains for each thread.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3138">Cada endereço nessa matriz fornece o local dos dados TLS para um determinado módulo (EXE ou DLL) dentro do programa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3138">Each address in this array gives the location of TLS data for a given module (EXE or DLL) within the program.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3139">O índice TLS indica qual membro da matriz deve ser usado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3139">The TLS index indicates which member of the array to use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3140">O índice é um número (significativo somente para o sistema) que identifica o módulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3140">The index is a number (meaningful only to the system) that identifies the module.</span></span>

#### <a name="the-tls-directory"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3141">O diretório TLS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3141">The TLS Directory</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3142">O diretório TLS tem o seguinte formato:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3142">The TLS directory has the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3143">Deslocamento (PE32/PE32 +)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3143">Offset (PE32/ PE32+)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3144">Tamanho (PE32/PE32 +)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3144">Size (PE32/ PE32+)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3145">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3145">Field</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3146">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3146">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
|----------------------|--------------------|----------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3147">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3147">0</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3148">4/8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3148">4/8</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3149">Início de dados brutos VA</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3149">Raw Data Start VA</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3150">O endereço inicial do modelo TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3150">The starting address of the TLS template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3151">O modelo é um bloco de dados que é usado para inicializar dados TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3151">The template is a block of data that is used to initialize TLS data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3152">O sistema copia todos esses dados sempre que um thread é criado, portanto, ele não deve estar corrompido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3152">The system copies all of this data each time a thread is created, so it must not be corrupted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3153">Observe que esse endereço não é um RVA; é um endereço para o qual deve haver uma realocação base na seção. realocação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3153">Note that this address is not an RVA; it is an address for which there should be a base relocation in the .reloc section.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3154">4/8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3154">4/8</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3155">4/8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3155">4/8</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3156">VA final de dados brutos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3156">Raw Data End VA</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3157">O endereço do último byte do TLS, exceto para o preenchimento zero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3157">The address of the last byte of the TLS, except for the zero fill.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3158">Assim como no campo data de início do VA, esse é um VA, não um RVA.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3158">As with the Raw Data Start VA field, this is a VA, not an RVA.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3159">8/16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3159">8/16</span></span> <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3160">4/8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3160">4/8</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3161">Endereço do índice</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3161">Address of Index</span></span> <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3162">O local para receber o índice TLS, que o carregador atribui.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3162">The location to receive the TLS index, which the loader assigns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3163">Esse local está em uma seção de dados comum, portanto, pode receber um nome simbólico acessível ao programa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3163">This location is in an ordinary data section, so it can be given a symbolic name that is accessible to the program.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                    |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3164">12/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3164">12/24</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3165">4/8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3165">4/8</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3166">Endereço de retornos de chamada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3166">Address of Callbacks</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3167">O ponteiro para uma matriz de funções de retorno de chamada TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3167">The pointer to an array of TLS callback functions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3168">A matriz é terminada em nulo, portanto, se não houver suporte para nenhuma função de retorno de chamada, esse campo apontará para 4 bytes definido como zero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3168">The array is null-terminated, so if no callback function is supported, this field points to 4 bytes set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3169">Para obter informações sobre o protótipo para essas funções, consulte [funções de retorno de chamada de TLS](#tls-callback-functions).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3169">For information about the prototype for these functions, see [TLS Callback Functions](#tls-callback-functions).</span></span><br/>                                                      |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3170">16/32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3170">16/32</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3171">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3171">4</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3172">Tamanho do preenchimento zero</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3172">Size of Zero Fill</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3173">O tamanho em bytes do modelo, além dos dados inicializados, delimitados pelos campos VA data de início e data final brutos de dados brutos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3173">The size in bytes of the template, beyond the initialized data delimited by the Raw Data Start VA and Raw Data End VA fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3174">O tamanho total do modelo deve ser igual ao tamanho total dos dados TLS no arquivo de imagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3174">The total template size should be the same as the total size of TLS data in the image file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3175">O preenchimento zero é a quantidade de dados que vem após os dados inicializados sem zero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3175">The zero fill is the amount of data that comes after the initialized nonzero data.</span></span> <br/>                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3176">20/36</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3176">20/36</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3177">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3177">4</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3178">Características</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3178">Characteristics</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3179">Os quatro bits \[ 23:20 \] descrevem as informações de alinhamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3179">The four bits \[23:20\] describe alignment info.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3180">Os valores possíveis são aqueles definidos como \_ \_ alinhamento \_ \* de SCN de imagem, que também são usados para descrever o alinhamento da seção em arquivos de objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3180">Possible values are those defined as IMAGE\_SCN\_ALIGN\_\*, which are also used to describe alignment of section in object files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3181">Os outros 28 bits são reservados para uso futuro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3181">The other 28 bits are reserved for future use.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                       |



 

#### <a name="tls-callback-functions"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3182">Funções de retorno de chamada TLS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3182">TLS Callback Functions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3183">O programa pode fornecer uma ou mais funções de retorno de chamada TLS para dar suporte à inicialização e terminação adicionais para objetos de dados TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3183">The program can provide one or more TLS callback functions to support additional initialization and termination for TLS data objects.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3184">Um uso típico para tal função de retorno de chamada seria chamar construtores e destruidores para objetos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3184">A typical use for such a callback function would be to call constructors and destructors for objects.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3185">Embora normalmente não haja mais de uma função de retorno de chamada, um retorno de chamada é implementado como uma matriz para possibilitar a adição de funções de retorno de chamada adicionais, se desejado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3185">Although there is typically no more than one callback function, a callback is implemented as an array to make it possible to add additional callback functions if desired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3186">Se houver mais de uma função de retorno de chamada, cada função será chamada na ordem em que seu endereço aparece na matriz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3186">If there is more than one callback function, each function is called in the order in which its address appears in the array.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3187">Um ponteiro nulo encerra a matriz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3187">A null pointer terminates the array.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3188">É perfeitamente válido ter uma lista vazia (nenhum retorno de chamada com suporte); nesse caso, a matriz de retorno de chamada tem exatamente um membro-um ponteiro nulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3188">It is perfectly valid to have an empty list (no callback supported), in which case the callback array has exactly one member-a null pointer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3189">O protótipo de uma função de retorno de chamada (apontado por um ponteiro do tipo \_ retorno de chamada PIMAGE TLS \_ ) tem os mesmos parâmetros que uma função de ponto de entrada de dll:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3189">The prototype for a callback function (pointed to by a pointer of type PIMAGE\_TLS\_CALLBACK) has the same parameters as a DLL entry-point function:</span></span>


```C++
typedef VOID
(NTAPI *PIMAGE_TLS_CALLBACK) (
    PVOID DllHandle,
    DWORD Reason,
    PVOID Reserved
    );
```



<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3190">O parâmetro reservado deve ser definido como zero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3190">The Reserved parameter should be set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3191">O parâmetro Reason pode assumir os seguintes valores:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3191">The Reason parameter can take the following values:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3192">Configuração</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3192">Setting</span></span>                          | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3193">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3193">Value</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3194">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3194">Description</span></span>                                                                                          |
|----------------------------------|---------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3195">\_anexar processo de dll \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3195">DLL\_PROCESS\_ATTACH</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3196">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3196">1</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3197">Um novo processo foi iniciado, incluindo o primeiro thread.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3197">A new process has started, including the first thread.</span></span> <br/>                                   |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3198">\_anexação de thread de dll \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3198">DLL\_THREAD\_ATTACH</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3199">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3199">2</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3200">Um novo thread foi criado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3200">A new thread has been created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3201">Essa notificação é enviada para todos, exceto para o primeiro thread.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3201">This notification sent for all but the first thread.</span></span> <br/>      |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3202">desanexação de thread de DLL \_ \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3202">DLL\_THREAD\_DETACH</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3203">3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3203">3</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3204">Um thread está prestes a ser encerrado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3204">A thread is about to be terminated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3205">Essa notificação é enviada para todos, exceto para o primeiro thread.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3205">This notification sent for all but the first thread.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3206">desanexar processo de DLL \_ \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3206">DLL\_PROCESS\_DETACH</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3207">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3207">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3208">Um processo está prestes a terminar, incluindo o thread original.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3208">A process is about to terminate, including the original thread.</span></span> <br/>                          |



 

### <a name="the-load-configuration-structure-image-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3209">A estrutura de configuração de carregamento (somente imagem)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3209">The Load Configuration Structure (Image Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3210">A estrutura de configuração de carregamento (diretório de configuração de carregamento de imagem \_ \_ \_ ) foi usada anteriormente em casos muito limitados no próprio sistema operacional Windows NT para descrever vários recursos muito difíceis ou muito grandes para descrever no cabeçalho do arquivo ou no cabeçalho opcional da imagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3210">The load configuration structure (IMAGE\_LOAD\_CONFIG\_DIRECTORY) was formerly used in very limited cases in the Windows NT operating system itself to describe various features too difficult or too large to describe in the file header or optional header of the image.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3211">As versões atuais do Microsoft linker e do Windows XP e versões posteriores do Windows usam uma nova versão desta estrutura para sistemas baseados em x86 de 32 bits que incluem a tecnologia SEH reservada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3211">Current versions of the Microsoft linker and Windows XP and later versions of Windows use a new version of this structure for 32-bit x86-based systems that include reserved SEH technology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3212">Isso fornece uma lista de manipuladores de exceção estruturados seguros que o sistema operacional usa durante a expedição de exceção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3212">This provides a list of safe structured exception handlers that the operating system uses during exception dispatching.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3213">Se o endereço do manipulador residir no intervalo de VA da imagem e estiver marcado como reconhecimento de SEH reservado (ou seja, a imagem \_ DLLCHARACTERISTICS \_ nenhum \_ Seh está clara no campo DLLCHARACTERISTICS do cabeçalho opcional, conforme descrito anteriormente), o manipulador deverá estar na lista de manipuladores confiáveis conhecidos para essa imagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3213">If the handler address resides in an image's VA range and is marked as reserved SEH-aware (that is, IMAGE\_DLLCHARACTERISTICS\_NO\_SEH is clear in the DllCharacteristics field of the optional header, as described earlier), then the handler must be in the list of known safe handlers for that image.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3214">Caso contrário, o sistema operacional encerrará o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3214">Otherwise, the operating system terminates the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3215">Isso ajuda a evitar a exploração de "seqüestro de manipulador de exceção x86" que foi usada no passado para assumir o controle do sistema operacional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3215">This helps prevent the "x86 exception handler hijacking" exploit that has been used in the past to take control of the operating system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3216">O Microsoft linker fornece automaticamente uma estrutura de configuração de carregamento padrão para incluir os dados de SEH reservados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3216">The Microsoft linker automatically provides a default load configuration structure to include the reserved SEH data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3217">Se o código de usuário já fornecer uma estrutura de configuração de carregamento, ele deverá incluir os novos campos de SEH reservados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3217">If the user code already provides a load configuration structure, it must include the new reserved SEH fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3218">Caso contrário, o vinculador não poderá incluir os dados SEH reservados e a imagem não será marcada como contendo SEH reservado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3218">Otherwise, the linker cannot include the reserved SEH data and the image is not marked as containing reserved SEH.</span></span>

#### <a name="load-configuration-directory"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3219">Carregar diretório de configuração</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3219">Load Configuration Directory</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3220">A entrada do diretório de dados para uma estrutura de configuração de carga SEH semireservada deve especificar um tamanho específico da estrutura de configuração de carga porque o carregador do sistema operacional sempre espera que seja um determinado valor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3220">The data directory entry for a pre-reserved SEH load configuration structure must specify a particular size of the load configuration structure because the operating system loader always expects it to be a certain value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3221">Nesse sentido, o tamanho é, na verdade, apenas uma verificação de versão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3221">In that regard, the size is really only a version check.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3222">Para compatibilidade com o Windows XP e versões anteriores do Windows, o tamanho deve ser 64 para imagens x86.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3222">For compatibility with Windows XP and earlier versions of Windows, the size must be 64 for x86 images.</span></span>

#### <a name="load-configuration-layout"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3223">Carregar layout de configuração</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3223">Load Configuration Layout</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3224">A estrutura de configuração de carregamento tem o seguinte layout para arquivos PE de 32 bits e de 64 bits:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3224">The load configuration structure has the following layout for 32-bit and 64-bit PE files:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3225">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3225">Offset</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3226">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3226">Size</span></span>            | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3227">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3227">Field</span></span>                                      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3228">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3228">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
|---------------------|-----------------|--------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3229">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3229">0</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3230">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3230">4</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3231">Características</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3231">Characteristics</span></span> <br/>                | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3232">Sinalizadores que indicam os atributos do arquivo, atualmente não utilizados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3232">Flags that indicate attributes of the file, currently unused.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3233">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3233">4</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3234">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3234">4</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3235">TimeDateStamp</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3235">TimeDateStamp</span></span> <br/>                  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3236">Valor de carimbo de data e hora.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3236">Date and time stamp value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3237">O valor é representado no número de segundos decorridos desde a meia-noite (00:00:00), 1º de janeiro de 1970, horário coordenado universal, de acordo com o relógio do sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3237">The value is represented in the number of seconds that have elapsed since midnight (00:00:00), January 1, 1970, Universal Coordinated Time, according to the system clock.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3238">O carimbo de data/hora pode ser impresso usando a função de tempo C Runtime (CRT).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3238">The time stamp can be printed by using the C runtime (CRT) time function.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3239">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3239">8</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3240">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3240">2</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3241">MajorVersion</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3241">MajorVersion</span></span> <br/>                   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3242">Número de versão principal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3242">Major version number.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
