<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3352">O campo GuardFlags contém uma combinação de um ou mais dos seguintes sinalizadores e subcampos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3352">The GuardFlags field contains a combination of one or more of the following flags and subfields:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3353">O módulo executa verificações de integridade de fluxo de controle usando o suporte fornecido pelo sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3353">Module performs control flow integrity checks using system-supplied support.</span></span>

    ` #define IMAGE_GUARD_CF_INSTRUMENTED  0x00000100`

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3354">O módulo executa o fluxo de controle e as verificações de integridade de gravação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3354">Module performs control flow and write integrity checks.</span></span>

    ` #define IMAGE_GUARD_CFW_INSTRUMENTED  0x00000200`

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3355">O módulo contém metadados de destino de fluxo de controle válidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3355">Module contains valid control flow target metadata.</span></span>

    `#define IMAGE_GUARD_CF_FUNCTION_TABLE_PRESENT  0x00000400`

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3356">O módulo não faz uso do cookie de segurança/GS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3356">Module does not make use of the /GS security cookie.</span></span>

    ` #define IMAGE_GUARD_SECURITY_COOKIE_UNUSED  0x00000800`

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3357">O módulo dá suporte à carga de atraso somente leitura IAT.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3357">Module supports read only delay load IAT.</span></span>

    `#define IMAGE_GUARD_PROTECT_DELAYLOAD_IAT  0x00001000`

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3358">DELAYLOAD importar tabela em sua própria seção. didat (com nada mais nele) que pode ser protegida livremente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3358">Delayload import table in its own .didat section (with nothing else in it) that can be freely reprotected.</span></span>

    ` #define IMAGE_GUARD_DELAYLOAD_IAT_IN_ITS_OWN_SECTION  0x00002000`

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3359">O módulo contém informações de exportação suprimidas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3359">Module contains suppressed export information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3360">Isso também infere que o endereço obtido pela tabela IAT também está presente na configuração de carga.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3360">This also infers that the address taken IAT table is also present in the load config.</span></span>

    `#define  IMAGE_GUARD_CF_EXPORT_SUPPRESSION_INFO_PRESENT  0x00004000`

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3361">O módulo permite a supressão de exportações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3361">Module enables suppression of exports.</span></span>

    `#define IMAGE_GUARD_CF_ENABLE_EXPORT_SUPPRESSION  0x00008000`

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3362">O módulo contém informações de destino do longjmp.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3362">Module contains longjmp target information.</span></span>

    ` #define IMAGE_GUARD_CF_LONGJUMP_TABLE_PRESENT  0x00010000`

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3363">Máscara do subcampo que contém o stride das entradas da tabela da função de proteção do fluxo de controle (ou seja, a contagem adicional de bytes por entrada de tabela).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3363">Mask for the subfield that contains the stride of Control Flow Guard function table entries (that is, the additional count of bytes per table entry).</span></span>

    ` #define IMAGE_GUARD_CF_FUNCTION_TABLE_SIZE_MASK  0xF0000000`

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3364">Além disso, o cabeçalho SDK do Windows Winnt. h define essa macro para a quantidade de bits a fim de deslocar o valor GuardFlags para justificar à direita a função de proteção de fluxo de controle Stride da tabela:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3364">Additionally, the Windows SDK winnt.h header defines this macro for the amount of bits to right-shift the GuardFlags value to right-justify the Control Flow Guard function table stride:</span></span>

` #define IMAGE_GUARD_CF_FUNCTION_TABLE_SIZE_SHIFT  28`

### <a name="the-rsrc-section"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3365">A seção. rsrc</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3365">The .rsrc Section</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3366">Os recursos são indexados por uma estrutura de árvore com classificação binária de vários níveis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3366">Resources are indexed by a multiple-level binary-sorted tree structure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3367">O design geral pode incorporar 2 \* \* 31 níveis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3367">The general design can incorporate 2\*\*31 levels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3368">Por convenção, no entanto, o Windows usa três níveis:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3368">By convention, however, Windows uses three levels:</span></span>

<dl> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3369">Tipo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3369">Type</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3370">Nome</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3370">Name</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3371">Idioma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3371">Language</span></span>  
</dl>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3372">Uma série de tabelas de diretório de recursos relaciona todos os níveis da seguinte maneira: cada tabela de diretório é seguida por uma série de entradas de diretório que fornecem o nome ou identificador (ID) para esse nível (tipo, nome ou nível de linguagem) e um endereço de uma descrição de dados ou outra tabela de diretório.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3372">A series of resource directory tables relates all of the levels in the following way: Each directory table is followed by a series of directory entries that give the name or identifier (ID) for that level (Type, Name, or Language level) and an address of either a data description or another directory table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3373">Se o endereço apontar para uma descrição de dados, os dados serão uma folha na árvore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3373">If the address points to a data description, then the data is a leaf in the tree.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3374">Se o endereço apontar para outra tabela de diretório, essa tabela listará as entradas de diretório no próximo nível abaixo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3374">If the address points to another directory table, then that table lists directory entries at the next level down.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3375">O tipo, o nome e as IDs de idioma de uma folha são determinados pelo caminho que é usado pelas tabelas de diretório para alcançar a folha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3375">A leaf's Type, Name, and Language IDs are determined by the path that is taken through directory tables to reach the leaf.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3376">A primeira tabela determina a ID de tipo, a segunda tabela (apontada pela entrada de diretório na primeira tabela) determina a ID de nome e a terceira tabela determina a ID de idioma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3376">The first table determines Type ID, the second table (pointed to by the directory entry in the first table) determines Name ID, and the third table determines Language ID.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3377">A estrutura geral da seção. rsrc é:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3377">The general structure of the .rsrc section is:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3378">Dados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3378">Data</span></span>                                                                   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3379">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3379">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3380">Tabelas de diretório de recursos (e entradas de diretório de recursos)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3380">Resource Directory Tables (and Resource Directory Entries)</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3381">Uma série de tabelas, uma para cada grupo de nós na árvore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3381">A series of tables, one for each group of nodes in the tree.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3382">Todos os nós de nível superior (tipo) são listados na primeira tabela.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3382">All top-level (Type) nodes are listed in the first table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3383">As entradas nesta tabela apontam para tabelas de segundo nível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3383">Entries in this table point to second-level tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3384">Cada árvore de segundo nível tem a mesma ID de tipo, mas IDs de nome diferentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3384">Each second-level tree has the same Type ID but different Name IDs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3385">Árvores de terceiro nível têm o mesmo tipo e IDs de nome, mas IDs de idioma diferentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3385">Third-level trees have the same Type and Name IDs but different Language IDs.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3386">Cada tabela individual é imediatamente seguida por entradas de diretório, nas quais cada entrada tem um nome ou identificador numérico e um ponteiro para uma descrição de dados ou uma tabela no nível inferior seguinte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3386">Each individual table is immediately followed by directory entries, in which each entry has a name or numeric identifier and a pointer to a data description or a table at the next lower level.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3387">Cadeias de caracteres do diretório de recursos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3387">Resource Directory Strings</span></span> <br/>                                 | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3388">Cadeias de caracteres Unicode alinhadas em dois bytes, que servem como dados de cadeias apontados por entradas de diretório.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3388">Two-byte-aligned Unicode strings, which serve as string data that is pointed to by directory entries.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3389">Descrição dos dados do recurso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3389">Resource Data Description</span></span> <br/>                                  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3390">Uma matriz de registros, apontada por tabelas, que descreve o tamanho real e o local dos dados do recurso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3390">An array of records, pointed to by tables, that describe the actual size and location of the resource data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3391">Esses registros são as folhas na árvore de descrição de recursos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3391">These records are the leaves in the resource-description tree.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3392">Dados de recurso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3392">Resource Data</span></span> <br/>                                              | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3393">Dados brutos da seção de recursos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3393">Raw data of the resource section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3394">As informações de tamanho e local no campo descrições de dados de recurso delimitam as regiões individuais dos dados do recurso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3394">The size and location information in the Resource Data Descriptions field delimit the individual regions of resource data.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |



 

#### <a name="resource-directory-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3395">Tabela de diretório de recursos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3395">Resource Directory Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3396">Cada tabela de diretório de recursos tem o formato a seguir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3396">Each resource directory table has the following format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3397">Essa estrutura de dados deve ser considerada o título de uma tabela porque a tabela realmente consiste em entradas de diretório (descritas na seção 6.9.2, "entradas do diretório de recursos") e esta estrutura:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3397">This data structure should be considered the heading of a table because the table actually consists of directory entries (described in section 6.9.2, "Resource Directory Entries") and this structure:</span></span>

#### <a name="resource-directory-entries"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3428">Entradas do diretório de recursos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3428">Resource Directory Entries</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3429">As entradas de diretório compõem as linhas de uma tabela.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3429">The directory entries make up the rows of a table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3430">Cada entrada do diretório de recursos tem o formato a seguir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3430">Each resource directory entry has the following format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3431">Se a entrada é um nome ou uma entrada de ID é indicada pela tabela de diretório de recursos, que indica quantas entradas de nome e ID são seguidas (Lembre-se de que todas as entradas de nome precedem todas as entradas de ID da tabela).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3431">Whether the entry is a Name or ID entry is indicated by the resource directory table, which indicates how many Name and ID entries follow it (remember that all the Name entries precede all the ID entries for the table).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3432">Todas as entradas da tabela são classificadas em ordem crescente: as entradas de nome por cadeia de caracteres que diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas e as entradas de ID por valor numérico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3432">All entries for the table are sorted in ascending order: the Name entries by case-sensitive string and the ID entries by numeric value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3433">Os deslocamentos são relativos ao endereço na entrada do \_ diretório de imagem \_ \_ DataDirectory de recursos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3433">Offsets are relative to the address in the IMAGE\_DIRECTORY\_ENTRY\_RESOURCE DataDirectory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3434">Consulte [emparelhamento dentro do PE: um tour do formato de arquivo executável portátil do Win32](/previous-versions/ms809762(v=msdn.10)#pe-file-resources) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3434">See [Peering Inside the PE: A Tour of the Win32 Portable Executable File Format](/previous-versions/ms809762(v=msdn.10)#pe-file-resources) for more information.</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3435">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3435">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3436">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3436">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3437">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3437">Field</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3438">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3438">Description</span></span>                                                                                                          |
|---------------|---------------|---------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3439">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3439">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3440">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3440">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3441">Deslocamento de nome</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3441">Name Offset</span></span> <br/>         | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3442">O deslocamento de uma cadeia de caracteres que fornece o tipo, o nome ou a entrada de ID de idioma, dependendo do nível da tabela.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3442">The offset of a string that gives the Type, Name, or Language ID entry, depending on level of table.</span></span> <br/>     |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3443">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3443">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3444">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3444">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3445">ID de inteiro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3445">Integer ID</span></span> <br/>          | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3446">Um inteiro de 32 bits que identifica o tipo, o nome ou a entrada de ID de idioma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3446">A 32-bit integer that identifies the Type, Name, or Language ID entry.</span></span> <br/>                                   |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3447">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3447">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3448">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3448">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3449">Deslocamento de entrada de dados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3449">Data Entry Offset</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3450">Alto bit 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3450">High bit 0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3451">Endereço de uma entrada de dados de recurso (uma folha).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3451">Address of a Resource Data entry (a leaf).</span></span> <br/>                                                   |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3452">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3452">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3453">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3453">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3454">Deslocamento de subdiretório</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3454">Subdirectory Offset</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3455">Alto bit 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3455">High bit 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3456">Os 31 bits inferiores são o endereço de outra tabela de diretório de recursos (o próximo nível abaixo).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3456">The lower 31 bits are the address of another resource directory table (the next level down).</span></span> <br/> |



 

#### <a name="resource-directory-string"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3457">Cadeia de caracteres do diretório de recursos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3457">Resource Directory String</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3458">A área de cadeia do diretório de recursos consiste em cadeias de caracteres Unicode, que são alinhadas ao Word.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3458">The resource directory string area consists of Unicode strings, which are word-aligned.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3459">Essas cadeias de caracteres são armazenadas juntas após a última entrada do diretório de recursos e antes da primeira entrada de dados do recurso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3459">These strings are stored together after the last Resource Directory entry and before the first Resource Data entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3460">Isso minimiza o impacto dessas cadeias de caracteres de comprimento variável no alinhamento das entradas de diretório de tamanho fixo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3460">This minimizes the impact of these variable-length strings on the alignment of the fixed-size directory entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3461">Cada cadeia de caracteres do diretório de recursos tem o seguinte formato:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3461">Each resource directory string has the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3462">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3462">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3463">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3463">Size</span></span>                 | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3464">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3464">Field</span></span>                      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3465">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3465">Description</span></span>                                                            |
|---------------|----------------------|----------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3466">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3466">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3467">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3467">2</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3468">Comprimento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3468">Length</span></span> <br/>         | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3469">O tamanho da cadeia de caracteres, não incluindo o próprio campo de comprimento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3469">The size of the string, not including length field itself.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3470">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3470">2</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3471">variável</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3471">variable</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3472">Cadeia de caracteres Unicode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3472">Unicode String</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3473">Os dados de cadeia de caracteres Unicode de comprimento variável, alinhados por palavra.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3473">The variable-length Unicode string data, word-aligned.</span></span> <br/>     |



 

#### <a name="resource-data-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3474">Entrada de dados do recurso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3474">Resource Data Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3475">Cada entrada de dados de recurso descreve uma unidade real de dados brutos na área de dados do recurso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3475">Each Resource Data entry describes an actual unit of raw data in the Resource Data area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3476">Uma entrada de dados de recurso tem o seguinte formato:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3476">A Resource Data entry has the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3477">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3477">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3478">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3478">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3479">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3479">Field</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3480">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3480">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                           |
|----------------|---------------|----------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3481">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3481">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3482">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3482">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3483">RVA de dados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3483">Data RVA</span></span> <br/>             | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3484">O endereço de uma unidade de dados de recurso na área de dados do recurso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3484">The address of a unit of resource data in the Resource Data area.</span></span> <br/>                                                                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3485">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3485">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3486">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3486">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3487">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3487">Size</span></span> <br/>                 | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3488">O tamanho, em bytes, dos dados de recurso que é apontado pelo campo RVA de dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3488">The size, in bytes, of the resource data that is pointed to by the Data RVA field.</span></span> <br/>                                                        |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3489">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3489">8</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3490">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3490">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3491">codepage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3491">Codepage</span></span> <br/>             | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3492">A página de código usada para decodificar valores de ponto de código dentro dos dados do recurso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3492">The code page that is used to decode code point values within the resource data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3493">Normalmente, a página de código seria a página de código Unicode.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3493">Typically, the code page would be the Unicode code page.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3494">12</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3494">12</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3495">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3495">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3496">Reservado, deve ser 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3496">Reserved, must be 0.</span></span> <br/> |                                                                                                                                                       |



 

### <a name="the-cormeta-section-object-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3497">A seção. cormeta (somente objeto)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3497">The .cormeta Section (Object Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3498">Os metadados CLR são armazenados nesta seção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3498">CLR metadata is stored in this section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3499">Ele é usado para indicar que o arquivo de objeto contém código gerenciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3499">It is used to indicate that the object file contains managed code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3500">O formato dos metadados não é documentado, mas pode ser enviado para as interfaces CLR para lidar com metadados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3500">The format of the metadata is not documented, but can be handed to the CLR interfaces for handling metadata.</span></span>

### <a name="the-sxdata-section"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3501">A seção. sxdata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3501">The .sxdata Section</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3502">Os manipuladores de exceção válidos de um objeto são listados na seção **. sxdata** desse objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3502">The valid exception handlers of an object are listed in the **.sxdata** section of that object.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3503">A seção está marcada como IMAGE \_ SCN \_ lnk \_ info.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3503">The section is marked IMAGE\_SCN\_LNK\_INFO.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3504">Ele contém o índice de símbolo COFF de cada manipulador válido, usando 4 bytes por índice.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3504">It contains the COFF symbol index of each valid handler, using 4 bytes per index.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3505">Além disso, o compilador marca um objeto COFF como SEH registrado emitindo o símbolo absoluto " @feat.00 " com o LSB do campo de valor definido como 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3505">Additionally, the compiler marks a COFF object as registered SEH by emitting the absolute symbol "@feat.00" with the LSB of the value field set to 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3506">Um objeto COFF sem manipuladores SEH registrados teria o @feat.00 símbolo "", mas não **. sxdata** seção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3506">A COFF object with no registered SEH handlers would have the "@feat.00" symbol, but no **.sxdata** section.</span></span>

## <a name="archive-library-file-format"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3507">Formato de arquivo de arquivamento (biblioteca)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3507">Archive (Library) File Format</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3508">Assinatura de arquivo morto</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3508">Archive File Signature</span></span>](#archive-file-signature)
- [<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3509">Arquivar cabeçalhos de membro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3509">Archive Member Headers</span></span>](#archive-member-headers)
- [<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3510">Primeiro membro do vinculador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3510">First Linker Member</span></span>](#first-linker-member)
- [<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3511">Segundo membro do vinculador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3511">Second Linker Member</span></span>](#second-linker-member)
- [<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3512">Membro longnames</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3512">Longnames Member</span></span>](#longnames-member)

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3513">O formato de arquivo COFF fornece um mecanismo padrão para armazenar coleções de arquivos de objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3513">The COFF archive format provides a standard mechanism for storing collections of object files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3514">Essas coleções são normalmente chamadas de bibliotecas na documentação de programação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3514">These collections are commonly called libraries in programming documentation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3515">Os primeiros 8 bytes de um arquivo consistem na assinatura do arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3515">The first 8 bytes of an archive consist of the file signature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3516">O restante do arquivo consiste em uma série de membros de arquivamento, da seguinte maneira:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3516">The rest of the archive consists of a series of archive members, as follows:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3517">O primeiro e o segundo Membros são "membros do vinculador".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3517">The first and second members are "linker members."</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3518">Cada um desses membros tem seu próprio formato, conforme descrito em seção [tipo de nome de importação](#import-name-type).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3518">Each of these members has its own format as described in section [Import Name Type](#import-name-type).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3519">Normalmente, um vinculador coloca informações nesses membros de arquivamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3519">Typically, a linker places information into these archive members.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3520">Os membros do vinculador contêm o diretório do arquivo morto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3520">The linker members contain the directory of the archive.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3521">O terceiro membro é o membro "longnames".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3521">The third member is the "longnames" member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3522">Esse membro opcional consiste em uma série de cadeias de caracteres ASCII com terminação nula em que cada cadeia de caracteres é o nome de outro membro de arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3522">This optional member consists of a series of null-terminated ASCII strings in which each string is the name of another archive member.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3523">O restante do arquivo consiste em membros padrão (arquivo de objeto).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3523">The rest of the archive consists of standard (object-file) members.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3524">Cada um desses membros contém o conteúdo de um arquivo de objeto em sua totalidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3524">Each of these members contains the contents of one object file in its entirety.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3525">Um cabeçalho de membro de arquivo precede cada membro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3525">An archive member header precedes each member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3526">A lista a seguir mostra a estrutura geral de um arquivo morto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3526">The following list shows the general structure of an archive:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3527">Assinatura: "! &lt; Arch &gt; \\ n "</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3527">Signature :"!&lt;arch&gt;\\n"</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3528">parâmetro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3528">Header</span></span>

    <dl> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3529">primeiro membro do vinculador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3529">1st Linker Member</span></span>  
    </dl>

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3530">parâmetro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3530">Header</span></span>

    <dl> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3531">2º membro do vinculador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3531">2nd Linker Member</span></span>  
    </dl>

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3532">parâmetro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3532">Header</span></span>

    <dl> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3533">Membro longnames</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3533">Longnames Member</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3534">parâmetro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3534">Header</span></span>

    <dl> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3535">Conteúdo do arquivo OBJ 1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3535">Contents of OBJ File 1</span></span>

### <a name="archive-file-signature"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3540">Assinatura de arquivo morto</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3540">Archive File Signature</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3541">A assinatura do arquivo morto identifica o tipo de arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3541">The archive file signature identifies the file type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3542">Qualquer utilitário (por exemplo, um vinculador) que usa um arquivo morto como entrada pode verificar o tipo de arquivo lendo essa assinatura.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3542">Any utility (for example, a linker) that takes an archive file as input can check the file type by reading this signature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3543">A assinatura consiste nos seguintes caracteres ASCII, nos quais cada caractere abaixo é representado literalmente, exceto pelo caractere de nova linha ( \\ n):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3543">The signature consists of the following ASCII characters, in which each character below is represented literally, except for the newline (\\n) character:</span></span>

`!<arch>\n`

### <a name="archive-member-headers"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3544">Arquivar cabeçalhos de membro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3544">Archive Member Headers</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3545">Cada membro (vinculador, longonames ou membro de arquivo de objeto) é precedido por um cabeçalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3545">Each member (linker, longnames, or object-file member) is preceded by a header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3546">Um cabeçalho de membro de arquivo tem o seguinte formato, no qual cada campo é uma cadeia de caracteres de texto ASCII que é justificada à esquerda e preenchida com espaços no final do campo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3546">An archive member header has the following format, in which each field is an ASCII text string that is left justified and padded with spaces to the end of the field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3547">Não há nenhum caractere nulo de encerramento em nenhum desses campos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3547">There is no terminating null character in any of these fields.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3548">Cada cabeçalho de membro começa no primeiro endereço par após o final do membro de arquivo anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3548">Each member header starts on the first even address after the end of the previous archive member.</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3549">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3549">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3550">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3550">Size</span></span>           | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3551">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3551">Field</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3552">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3552">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
|----------------|----------------|---------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3553">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3553">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3554">16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3554">16</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3555">Nome</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3555">Name</span></span> <br/>          | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3556">O nome do membro de arquivo, com uma barra (/) anexada para encerrar o nome.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3556">The name of the archive member, with a slash (/) appended to terminate the name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3557">Se o primeiro caractere for uma barra, o nome terá uma interpretação especial, conforme descrito na tabela a seguir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3557">If the first character is a slash, the name has a special interpretation, as described in the following table.</span></span> <br/> |

| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3562">28</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3562">28</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3563">6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3563">6</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3564">ID do Usuário</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3564">User ID</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3565">Uma representação decimal ASCII da ID de usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3565">An ASCII decimal representation of the user ID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3566">Esse campo não contém um valor significativo em plataformas do Windows porque as ferramentas da Microsoft emitem todos os espaços em branco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3566">This field does not contain a meaningful value on Windows platforms because Microsoft tools emit all blanks.</span></span> <br/>                                    |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3567">34</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3567">34</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3568">6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3568">6</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3569">ID do Grupo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3569">Group ID</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3570">Uma representação decimal ASCII da ID do grupo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3570">An ASCII decimal representation of the group ID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3571">Esse campo não contém um valor significativo em plataformas do Windows porque as ferramentas da Microsoft emitem todos os espaços em branco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3571">This field does not contain a meaningful value on Windows platforms because Microsoft tools emit all blanks.</span></span> <br/>                                   |

### <a name="first-linker-member"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3599">Primeiro membro do vinculador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3599">First Linker Member</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3600">O nome do primeiro membro do vinculador é "/".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3600">The name of the first linker member is "/".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3601">O primeiro membro do vinculador está incluído para compatibilidade com versões anteriores.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3601">The first linker member is included for backward compatibility.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3602">Ele não é usado por vinculadores atuais, mas seu formato deve estar correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3602">It is not used by current linkers, but its format must be correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3603">Esse membro do vinculador fornece um diretório de nomes de símbolo, assim como o segundo membro do vinculador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3603">This linker member provides a directory of symbol names, as does the second linker member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3604">Para cada símbolo, as informações indicam onde encontrar o membro de arquivo que contém o símbolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3604">For each symbol, the information indicates where to find the archive member that contains the symbol.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3605">O primeiro membro do vinculador tem o formato a seguir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3605">The first linker member has the following format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3606">Essas informações são exibidas após o cabeçalho:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3606">This information appears after the header:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3607">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3607">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3608">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3608">Size</span></span>               | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3609">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3609">Field</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3610">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3610">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
|----------------|--------------------|-------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3611">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3611">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3612">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3612">4</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3613">Número de símbolos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3613">Number of Symbols</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3614">O Long sem sinal que contém o número de símbolos indexados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3614">Unsigned long that contains the number of indexed symbols.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3615">Esse número é armazenado no formato big-endian.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3615">This number is stored in big-endian format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3616">Cada membro do arquivo de objeto normalmente define um ou mais símbolos externos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3616">Each object-file member typically defines one or more external symbols.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3617">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3617">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3618">4 \* n</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3618">4 \* n</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3619">Deslocamentos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3619">Offsets</span></span> <br/>           | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3620">Uma matriz de deslocamentos de arquivo para arquivar cabeçalhos de membro, em que n é igual ao campo número de símbolos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3620">An array of file offsets to archive member headers, in which n is equal to the Number of Symbols field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3621">Cada número na matriz é um Long não assinado armazenado no formato big endian.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3621">Each number in the array is an unsigned long stored in big-endian format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3622">Para cada símbolo que é nomeado na tabela de cadeia de caracteres, o elemento correspondente na matriz de deslocamentos fornece o local do membro de arquivo que contém o símbolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3622">For each symbol that is named in the string table, the corresponding element in the offsets array gives the location of the archive member that contains the symbol.</span></span> <br/> |
| \* <br/> | \* <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3623">Tabela de cadeias de caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3623">String Table</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3624">Uma série de cadeias de caracteres terminadas em nulo que nomeiem todos os símbolos no diretório.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3624">A series of null-terminated strings that name all the symbols in the directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3625">Cada cadeia de caracteres começa imediatamente após o caractere nulo na cadeia de caracteres anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3625">Each string begins immediately after the null character in the previous string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3626">O número de cadeias de caracteres deve ser igual ao valor do campo número de símbolos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3626">The number of strings must be equal to the value of the Number of Symbols field.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                       |



 

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3627">Os elementos na matriz de deslocamentos devem ser organizados em ordem crescente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3627">The elements in the offsets array must be arranged in ascending order.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3628">Esse fato significa que os símbolos na tabela de cadeia de caracteres devem ser organizados de acordo com a ordem dos membros de arquivamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3628">This fact implies that the symbols in the string table must be arranged according to the order of archive members.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3629">Por exemplo, todos os símbolos no primeiro membro do arquivo de objeto teriam que ser listados antes dos símbolos no segundo arquivo de objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3629">For example, all the symbols in the first object-file member would have to be listed before the symbols in the second object file.</span></span>

### <a name="second-linker-member"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3630">Segundo membro do vinculador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3630">Second Linker Member</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3631">O segundo membro do vinculador tem o nome "/" como o primeiro membro do vinculador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3631">The second linker member has the name "/" as does the first linker member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3632">Embora ambos os membros do vinculador forneçam um diretório de símbolos e membros de arquivo que os contêm, o segundo membro do vinculador é usado em preferência ao primeiro por todos os vinculadores atuais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3632">Although both linker members provide a directory of symbols and archive members that contain them, the second linker member is used in preference to the first by all current linkers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3633">O segundo membro do vinculador inclui nomes de símbolo na ordem lexical, o que permite uma pesquisa mais rápida por nome.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3633">The second linker member includes symbol names in lexical order, which enables faster searching by name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3634">O segundo membro tem o formato a seguir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3634">The second member has the following format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3635">Essas informações são exibidas após o cabeçalho:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3635">This information appears after the header:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3636">Deslocamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3636">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3637">Tamanho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3637">Size</span></span>               | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3638">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3638">Field</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3639">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3639">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
|----------------|--------------------|-------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3640">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3640">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3641">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3641">4</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3642">Número de membros</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3642">Number of Members</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3643">Um Long sem sinal que contém o número de membros de arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3643">An unsigned long that contains the number of archive members.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |

| \* <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3650">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3650">4</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3651">Número de símbolos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3651">Number of Symbols</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3652">Um Long sem sinal que contém o número de símbolos indexados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3652">An unsigned long that contains the number of symbols indexed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3653">Cada membro do arquivo de objeto normalmente define um ou mais símbolos externos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3653">Each object-file member typically defines one or more external symbols.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| \* <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3654">2 \* n</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3654">2 \* n</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3655">Índices</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3655">Indices</span></span> <br/>           | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3656">Uma matriz de índices baseados em 1 (sem sinal curto) que mapeia nomes de símbolos para arquivar deslocamentos de membro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3656">An array of 1-based indexes (unsigned short ) that map symbol names to archive member offsets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3657">O número n é igual ao número de símbolos do campo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3657">The number n is equal to the Number of Symbols field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3658">Para cada símbolo que é nomeado na tabela de cadeia de caracteres, o elemento correspondente na matriz de índices fornece um índice para a matriz de deslocamentos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3658">For each symbol that is named in the string table, the corresponding element in the Indices array gives an index into the offsets array.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3659">A matriz de deslocamentos, por sua vez, fornece o local do membro de arquivo que contém o símbolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3659">The offsets array, in turn, gives the location of the archive member that contains the symbol.</span></span> <br/> |
| \* <br/> | \* <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3660">Tabela de cadeias de caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3660">String Table</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3661">Uma série de cadeias de caracteres terminadas em nulo que nomeiem todos os símbolos no diretório.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3661">A series of null-terminated strings that name all of the symbols in the directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3662">Cada cadeia de caracteres começa imediatamente após o byte nulo na cadeia de caracteres anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3662">Each string begins immediately after the null byte in the previous string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3663">O número de cadeias de caracteres deve ser igual ao valor do campo número de símbolos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3663">The number of strings must be equal to the value of the Number of Symbols field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3664">Esta tabela lista todos os nomes de símbolo em ordem lexical crescente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3664">This table lists all the symbol names in ascending lexical order.</span></span> <br/>                                                                             |



 

### <a name="longnames-member"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3665">Membro longnames</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3665">Longnames Member</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3666">O nome do membro longnames é "//".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3666">The name of the longnames member is "//".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3667">O membro longnames é uma série de cadeias de caracteres de nomes de membro de arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3667">The longnames member is a series of strings of archive member names.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3668">Um nome aparece aqui somente quando não há espaço suficiente no campo nome (16 bytes).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3668">A name appears here only when there is insufficient room in the Name field (16 bytes).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3669">O membro longnames é opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3669">The longnames member is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3670">Ele pode estar vazio com apenas um cabeçalho ou pode estar completamente ausente sem até mesmo um cabeçalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3670">It can be empty with only a header, or it can be completely absent without even a header.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3671">As cadeias de caracteres são terminadas em nulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3671">The strings are null-terminated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3672">Cada cadeia de caracteres começa imediatamente após o byte nulo na cadeia de caracteres anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3672">Each string begins immediately after the null byte in the previous string.</span></span>

## <a name="import-library-format"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3673">Importar formato de biblioteca</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3673">Import Library Format</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3674">Importar cabeçalho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3674">Import Header</span></span>](#import-header)
- [<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3675">Tipo de importação</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3675">Import Type</span></span>](#import-type)

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3676">Bibliotecas de importação tradicionais, ou seja, bibliotecas que descrevem as exportações de uma imagem para uso por outra, normalmente seguem o layout descrito na seção 7, [formato de arquivo morto (biblioteca)](#archive-library-file-format).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3676">Traditional import libraries, that is, libraries that describe the exports from one image for use by another, typically follow the layout described in section 7, [Archive (Library) File Format](#archive-library-file-format).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3677">A principal diferença é que os membros da biblioteca de importação contêm arquivos pseudo-objeto em vez de verdadeiros, em que cada membro inclui as contribuições de seção necessárias para criar as tabelas de importação que são descritas na seção 6,4, [a seção. iData](#the-idata-section) o vinculador gera esse arquivo ao compilar o aplicativo de exportação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3677">The primary difference is that import library members contain pseudo-object files instead of real ones, in which each member includes the section contributions that are required to build the import tables that are described in section 6.4, [The .idata Section](#the-idata-section) The linker generates this archive while building the exporting application.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3678">As contribuições de seção para uma importação podem ser inferidas de um pequeno conjunto de informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3678">The section contributions for an import can be inferred from a small set of information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3679">O vinculador pode gerar as informações completas e detalhadas na biblioteca de importação para cada membro no momento da criação da biblioteca ou gravar apenas as informações canônicas na biblioteca e permitir que o aplicativo que o usa posteriormente gere os dados necessários em tempo real.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3679">The linker can either generate the complete, verbose information into the import library for each member at the time of the library's creation or write only the canonical information to the library and let the application that later uses it generate the necessary data on the fly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3680">Em uma biblioteca de importação com o formato longo, um único membro contém as seguintes informações:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3680">In an import library with the long format, a single member contains the following information:</span></span>

<dl> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3681">Cabeçalho de membro de arquivo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3681">Archive member header</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3682">Cabeçalho do arquivo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3682">File header</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3683">Cabeçalhos de seção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3683">Section headers</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3684">Dados que correspondem a cada um dos cabeçalhos de seção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3684">Data that corresponds to each of the section headers</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3685">Tabela de símbolos COFF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3685">COFF symbol table</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3686">Cadeias de caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3686">Strings</span></span>  
  
</dl>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3687">Por outro lado, uma biblioteca de importação curta é escrita da seguinte maneira:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3687">In contrast, a short import library is written as follows:</span></span>

<dl> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3688">Cabeçalho de membro de arquivo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3688">Archive member header</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3689">Importar cabeçalho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3689">Import header</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3690">Cadeia de nome de importação terminada em nulo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3690">Null-terminated import name string</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3691">Cadeia de caracteres de nome de DLL terminada em nulo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3691">Null-terminated DLL name string</span></span>  
</dl>

<span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3692">Essas são informações suficientes para reconstruir com precisão todo o conteúdo do membro no momento de seu uso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3692">This is sufficient information to accurately reconstruct the entire contents of the member at the time of its use.</span></span>

|                | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3734">3 bits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3734">3 bits</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3735">Tipo de nome</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3735">Name Type</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3736">O tipo de nome de importação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3736">The import name type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cbc1-3737">Para obter mais informações, consulte [importar tipo de nome](#import-name-type).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cbc1-3737">For more information, see [Import Name Type](#import-name-type).</span></span> <br/>                           |
